# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

# etcd MVCC Compaction and Watch Stream Cancellation

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in etcd-io/etcd that implement MVCC compaction: the compaction schedule (periodic vs revision-based), the compaction of revision indices, the notification of watch streams that span a compacted revision, and the slow watch detection.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

68-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the MVCC compaction implementation in etcd. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings

I've created a detailed JSON file at `/workspace/answer.json` that documents all relevant Go source files implementing:

### 1. **Compaction Scheduling (Periodic vs Revision-based)**
- **Periodic**: Tracks revisions every 1/10th of retention period, compacts after retention elapses
- **Revision-based**: Compacts every 5 minutes based on `currentRevision - retentionCount`
- Both implemented as separate types with identical interfaces for `Run()`, `Stop()`, `Pause()`, `Resume()`

### 2. **Compaction of Revision Indices**
- **Key Index Compaction** (`key_index.go:doCompact`): Removes old revisions from per-key generation records
- **Backend Compaction** (`kvstore_compaction.go:scheduleCompaction`): Batch-deletes entries from backend storage
- Uses configurable batch limits and sleep intervals

### 3. **Notification of Watch Streams Spanning Compacted Revisions**
- **Critical path**: `watcher_group.go:chooseAll()` sends `CompactRevision` notification to watchers with `minRev < compactRev`
- **Synchronization**: `watchable_store.go:syncWatchers()` retrieves events and handles blocked watchers
- **Victim Management**: Unsynced watchers that can't receive events are retried every 10ms

### 4. **Slow Watch Detection**
- **Metrics**: `slowWatcherGauge` tracks unsynced slow watchers, `pendingEventsGauge` tracks events awaiting delivery
- **Detection**: Watches that fall behind current revision are marked as "victims" and tracked separately
- **Recovery**: Gauges are updated as slow watchers catch up

### 5. **Server Integration**
- Compactor is instantiated and managed by `EtcdServer` 
- Runs as background goroutine, receives compacti
... (truncated)

(Multi-Version Concurrency Control) compaction involves periodic cleanup of old revisions and intelligent management of watch streams that span compacted revisions. The following describes the key components:\\n\\n### 1. Compaction Scheduling: Periodic vs Revision-based\\n\\nCompaction is scheduled through two modes configured via `--auto-compaction-mode`:\\n\\n**Periodic Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go:Periodic`):\\n- Records revisions periodically (every 1/10th of the retention period)\\n- Executes compaction after the retention period has elapsed\\n- For retention periods < 1 hour: compacts every X hours (e.g., 10m retention \u2192 compact every 10m)\\n- For retention periods \u2265 1 hour: compacts every 1 hour\\n- Implements exponential backoff retry on failure (lines 100-163)\\n\\n**Revision-based Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go:Revision`):\\n- Compacts at a fixed interval (5 minutes via `revInterval`)\\n- Retains a specified number of revisions from the current maximum revision\\n- Calculates: `compactionRev = currentRev - retention` (lines 64-112)\\n\\nBoth implementations are created through the factory pattern in `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/compactor.go:New()` (lines 55-73), which routes to either periodic or revision-based compaction.\\n\\n### 2. Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\n**Index Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/key_index.go`):\\n- The `Compact()` method on `keyIndex` removes old revisions of keys\\n- Processes the `generations` structure (lines 44-72 in key_index.go comments) which tracks key mutations\\n- `doCompact()` (lines 258-282) walks through key generations and removes revisions <= compactionRev\\n- Maintains `available` map to track which revisions should be kept\\n\\n**Backend Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go:scheduleCompaction`):\\n- Iterates through backend storage in batches (lines 42-99)\\n- Deletes entries with revisions that are not in the `keep` map (generated from index compaction)\\n- Uses configurable batch limits via `CompactionBatchLimit` and sleep intervals via `CompactionSleepInterval`\\n- Records metrics: `indexCompactionPauseMs`, `dbCompactionTotalMs`, `dbCompactionKeysCounter`, `dbCompactionLast`\\n\\n### 3. Notification of Watch Streams Spanning Compacted Revisions\\n\\nWhen a watcher's minimum revision falls below the compaction revision, it must be notified:\\n\\n**Watch Stream Cancellation** (`server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go:chooseAll`, lines 237-266):\\n- During sync of unsynced watchers, `chooseAll()` checks if `w.minRev < compactRev`\\n- Sends a `WatchResponse` with `CompactRevision: compactRev` (line 253)\\n- Marks the watcher as `compacted = true` (line 254)\\n- Removes the watcher from the group (line 255)\\n- This notification tells clients their watch window has been compacted away\\n\\n**Watch Synchronization** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go:syncWatchers`, lines 346-414):\\n- Unsynced watchers are synced in batches (maxWatchersPerSync = 512)\\n- Retrieves events from current store state and sends to watchers\\n- Watches that couldn't send due to full channels become \\\"victims\\\" (lines 390-405)\\n- Calls `slowWatcherGauge.Set()` to track slow watchers (line 411)\\n\\n**Victim Handling** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go:moveVictims` and `syncVictimsLoop`, lines 257-339):\\n- Maintains a list of blocked watchers (\\\"victims\\\") that couldn't receive events\\n- Retries sending events to victims every 10ms (line 272)\\n- Once successfully sent, moves watchers back to synced/unsynced groups\\n- Decrements `slowWatcherGauge` when a slow watcher is no longer slow (line 324)\\n\\n### 4. Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nSlow watchers (watchers that fall behind) are tracked and managed:\\n\\n**Metrics** (`server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go`):\\n- `slowWatcherGauge` (lines 87-94): Tracks total number of unsynced slow watchers\\n- `pendingEventsGauge` (lines 105-112): Tracks pending events awaiting delivery\\n- Updated during `syncWatchers()` at line 411 of watchable_store.go\\n\\n**Detection Mechanism** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go`):\\n- When a watcher's channel is full (can't send), it's marked as `victim = true` (line 505)\\n- The slow watcher gauge is incremented (line 508) when moved to unsynced\\n- The gauge is decremented (line 324) when the watcher recovers\\n- Slow watchers are defined as unsynced watchers that haven't caught up to current revision\\n\\n### 5.
